ṣoḍaśāhutirjuhuyāt | etadvayaṃ vaktaiva karaṇaṃ nāḍīsaṃdhānaṃ | tatastri   
madhurāktaṃ raktakaravīrairvā anyena vā aṣṭottaraśataṃ nityahome | bandhūka   
kusumai bhūpavasyāya | sarpilavaṇahomābhyāṃ kāminī samākarṣaṇāya |  
  
p. 170a)  
  
candana puṣpaiḥ saubhāgyāya | mallikājātī punnāga kadambaiḥ puṣpairājakusumai   
sarvārtha siddhai | durvātilājyāhutirāmuṣe | kṣīrāktaistagaraiḥ kavitvāya |   
candanāgurukarpuraiḥ sarvābhiṣṭāya ghṛtāktamālatīpuṣpai druta kavitvāya |   
puraścaraṇavidhau tu |  
  
nīlotpalenākhaṇḍāya bilvapatreṇa vā daśāṃmaśaṃjuhūyāt | vahuraprakārastu   
mūlamuccārya tataḥ svāhā |  
  
p. 170b)  
  
idaṃ devyai tataḥ punarmahāvyāhriti homayet | yathā |  
  
oṃ bhūragnaye pṛthivyai mahate svāhā | bhuvo vāyave cāntarikṣāya ca dive ca   
mahate svahā | oṃ svaḥ ādityāya candramase nakṣatrebhyaśca vai svāhā |  
oṃ bhūrbhuvaḥ sva agnaye cādityāya candramase nakṣetrebhyañca mahate svāhā |  
  
iti hutvā ārjyapūrṇena śuvena śruvamāpūjya tatrākṣata kusumā niḥkṣipet |   
tadupari adhomukha śuva datvā urddhaṃ mūkhena mūlaṃ nādāntamūccārya   
vāmapādapūraḥsaraṃ ||  
  
p. 171a)  
  
avichinnadhārayā vauṣaḍantena pūrṇāhutiṃ hutvā upaviśya devī   
gaṃdhādibhirārādhya tadaṃta devatā gaṇaṃ tadaṃmeva ca |  
  
vilīnaṃ dhyātvā pūrvavat visarjayet | śaktaścet saṃrakṣet |  
  
atha haviṣyānnavidhi |  
  
mantrānte svāhākāramuccāryadvavirnnikṣipyānte idamamūkāyeti sambandhaḥ |   
havirdānantunpūnjapāninā na kartavyaṃ | taduktaṃ tripurāntahāre |  
  
citrahastena yaddānaṃ huyate ca hutāśane |  
  
p. 171b)  
  
dātu punyaphalaṃ nāsti hotā ca narakaṃ vrajet ||  
  
iti śrīmahābhairavatantre |  
  
havirūtāna hastena vaiśvānara mukhe hutaṃ |  
hotuścakṣurvināśāya yajamānopi naśyati ||  
  
iti tārārahasyavṛttau homanirṇayo nāmaḥ trayodaśaḥ paṭalaḥ || 13 ||  
  
  
evaṃ nigaditā vidyā tāriṇī sarvasiddhidā |  
idānīṃ śṛṇu vakṣāmi vāsanāmātmatāmayīṃ ||  
  
vyomno prakāśamānastvaṃ rasannāyatramagninā |  
tayorviṣa ikāroyaṃ vidūnā tantrikā matā ||  
  
p. 172a)  
  
takāra sarvapāpaghno rephastatva prakāśakaḥ |  
bindūmānī mahābījaṃ śabdarāśeḥ prakāśakaṃ ||  
  
caitanyarūpa saṃsārabhīṣaṇaṃ muktidāyakaṃ |  
phatkāra sarvajāḍyānāṃ nāśakaṃ tatprakāśakaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ samastarūpeṇa kevalā citkalāparā |  
sarvavedamayī sākṣāchabdabrahmaśvarūpiṇī ||  
  
ānandarūpiṇī nīlā ātmānanda pradāyiṇī |  
praṇavo brahmarūpāsā sohaṃ tatva svarūpiṇī ||  
  
p. 172b)  
  
iti te kathitā vidyā vāsanā bhuktimukti ye |  
evaṃ yo vetti śuddhātmā sādhako guru śikṣayā ||  
  
sa yogī sa ca vijñānī jīvaṃ muktaḥ sadāśivaḥ |  
  
atha mantrasiddhyartha maṃtra śikhāmahārahasyatantre |  
  
śrīdevyuvāca |  
  
bhagavan prasīda sarvajña sarvaprāṇi hiterata |  
yenāvaśya bhave siddhiḥ rūpāya vada śaṃkaraḥ ||  
  
śrī īśvara uvāca |  
  
śṛṇu devi paraṃ jñānaṃ sarva jñānottamottamaṃ |  
yena vijñātamātreṇa kṣipraṃ vidyā prasīdati ||  
  
p. 173a)  
  
mūlakalpe tu yā śaktirbhujaṃgākāra rūpiṇī |  
etadarbhanāvartana praṇa ityucyate budhaiḥ ||  
  
jhillivāracya madhurā krūjandī satato sthitā |  
gachantī brahmaraṃdhre praviśanti svaketana ||  
  
yātāyātaṃ krameṇaiva tacca kūryāmanomayaṃ |  
tena mantra śikhājātā sarvasiddhi pradīpikā ||  
  
tamaḥ purṇe gṛhe yastu yatkiñcit pratibhāṣate |  
śikhā hīnāstathā mantrā na siddhyaṃti kadācana ||  
  
p. 173b)  
  
śikhopadeśaḥ sarvatra gopitaḥ parameśvaraḥ |  
vitānena na siddhi syāt varṣakoṭī śatairapi ||  
  
tasmāt tvayāpi girije gopitavyaṃ prayatnataḥ |  
  
iti śikhā mantrā | mantraśikhā | athāntaryāgaḥ | rudrayāmale |  
  
athāntaryejanaṃ vakṣe dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭa phalapradaṃ |  
yogiṇāṃ yatra jāyante adhipāśca narāḥ sadā ||  
  
gurodhyānaṃ prakūrvīta yatnāt pūrvaṃ viśāladhī |  
snānaṃ budhastataḥ kūrya svamvidānanda siddhaye ||  
  
p. 174a)  
  
tadyathā śṛṅgāta nilayā kuṇḍalinī samutthāpya kula paṃke ruhaṃ parabindūṃ   
niṅbhidya tatra druta parāmṛta dhārayā mūla śṛṅgāṃtargataṃ tatra nimajjet   
|   
  
taduktaṃ yāmale |  
  
snāyācca vimale tīrthe puṣkare hṛdayāśrite |  
bindutīrthe naraḥ snāyāt punarjanma na vidyate ||  
  
iḍāsuṣumnā śivatīrthakesmin jñānāmbu pūrṇā vahata śarīre |  
brahmadyuti snāti tayoḥ sadāyat kintasya gaṃgairapi puṣkaraiścaḥ ||  
  
p. 174b)  
  
atha saṃdhyā |  
  
mūlavidyāsvarūpiṇī taḍitkoṭi prabhāṃ mṛṇālatantu nibhāṃ kuṇḍalinīṃ   
kulāmṛtarasabhāvena saṃdhyā kūryāt |  
  
taduktaṃ rudrayāmale |  
  
śivaḥ śaktyāḥ samāyogo yasmijñāna prajāyate |  
sā saṃdhyā kulaniṣṭānāṃ samādhisthaiḥ pragīyate ||  
  
atha tarpaṇa |  
  
mūlādhārāt somasūryāgni rūpiṇīṃ kuṇḍalinīṃ samusthāpya paraṃ   
bindūnibhidyatadabhūtā mṛtena deha devatāṃ tarpayet para devatāṃ |  
  
p. 175a)  
  
athārgha vidhiḥ |  
  
bindusthānamādhāranādasthāne kalārūpapātraṃ nādānta   
candramaṇḍalāmṛtājñā cakraśuddhyā śaktitejasā saṃpūjya deha devatāṃ   
tarpayet | tarpanaiḥ taduktaṃ bhairave |  
  
brahmadvārā dadhobhāge taccāntaṃ pātramuttamaṃ |  
kāmāsāreṇa saṃpūjya tarpayantena khecarīṃ ||  
  
nyāsā yathā |  
  
ṣaṭcakrasthitā māttṛkānanī karaṃ nyāsaḥ |  
  
taduktaṃ rudrayāmale |  
  
p. 175b)  
  
ādhāre liṃganābhau hṛdaya sarasije tālumūle lalāṭe dve patre ṣoḍaśāre   
dvidaśa daśadale dvādaśārddha catuṣke |  
  
vāsānte vālamadhye upha kaṭha sahite kaṇṭhakūpe svarāśca haṃsaṃ tatvārtha   
yukte sakala dalagataṃ kaulamārga prasiddhiṃ |  
  
pāṭha hakṣau daḍamadhyenyasa tu vimaladhīrṣūddhi saṃmanti vṛdyai |  
  
atha ṣaḍaṃgāni gotamīye |  
  
iḍyamānā hṛdānmānaṃ hṛdaye syārcidātmakaṃḥ |  
  
p. 176a)  
  
kriye tatparatvena hṛnmayena tataḥ paraṃ |  
sarvajñādi guṇottuṃge sarve hrī& ca parānmani ||  
  
kriyati viṣayāhāro śiromantreṇa deśikaḥ |  
hṛchiro rūpaḥ ciddhāma mayamābhāvanādṛḍham ||  
  
kriyate nija devasya śikhāmantreṇa deśakaḥ |  
mantrātmakasya dehasya mantravācyena tejasā ||  
  
sarvatovarmamantreṇa kriyate nānyamanvati |  
yaṅgatādi parajñānamanvirūpe parātmani ||  
  
hṛdayādi mayaṃ tejaḥ syādai tat netra saṃjñitaṃ |  
  
p. 176b)  
  
andhyātmikādi rūpaṃ yat sādhakasya vināśayet ||  
  
avidyā jātamantrasya paraṃ dhāma samīritaṃ |  
  
atha dhyānaṃ |  
  
tadūktaṃ udayākarapaddhatyāṃ |  
  
śaktidvaya puṭāntastha kamaladvaya saṃsthitaṃ |  
jyotistatvamaya dhyātvā kulākula viyojanaṃ ||  
  
śṛṅgāṭadvayamadhyasthaṃ śaktidvaya puṭī kṛtaṃ |  
sadāsamarasandhyānantatkulaṃ yoginī mayi ||  
  
punaruktaṃ |  
  
kiraṇasthaṃ yadāgnisthañcandra bhāskara madhyagaṃ |  
  
p. 177a)  
  
mahāśūnye layaṃ kṛtvā purṇastiṣṭati yogirāt ||  
  
nilālamba pade śūnye yat teja upajāyate |  
tad garbhamabhyasennityandhyānamevantu yogiṇāṃ ||  
  
atha pūjā | yathā |  
  
antarmukhena manasā viṣayādikaṃ sarva paratejasi samarpaṇamiti pūjanaṃ |   
taduktaṃ bhairava tantre |  
  
arcayaṃ viṣayaiḥ puṣpaistatkṣaṇāntatmayo bhavet |  
  
anyatrāpi |  
  
nyāsastatmayatā buddhiḥ sohaṃ bhāvena pūjayet |  
  
p. 177b)  
  
atha japau yathā |  
  
suṣumnāntargataṃ cichakti rupabrahmagranthisūtra granthitasya   
merusamanvitānulomavilomena kuṇḍaliṇīmutthāpya japet |  
  
taduktaṃ mātṛkārṇave |  
  
mālā pañcāsikā proktā sutraṃ śakti śivātmakaṃ |  
granthitaṃ kūṇḍalī śakti kalānte meru saṃsthitāḥ ||  
  
atha homaḥ |  
  
nābhikūṇḍe kuṇḍalinī vidagnau vāsanendhane dīpte parāmṛta haviṣu sumnā   
śruvā |  
  
p. 178a)  
  
akṣavṛttīrvakṣamāṇamantreṇa juhūyāt |  
  
mantro yathā |  
  
mūlamuccāryanābhimaṇḍalacaitanyarūpāgnau manasā śruvā jñāna pradīpake   
nilamakṣaravṛttījuhomyahaṃ |  
  
svāhā ityekāhutiṃ datvā mūlamūccārya |  
dharmādharma havīrdvipta rūpāgnau manasā śruvā ||  
  
suṣumnāvartmanā nityamakṣavṛtti juhomyahaṃ |  
svāhā iti dvitīyāhutiḥ ||  
  
mūlamūcāryā |  
  
prakāśākāśahastābhyāṃ havanaṃ ātmano śruvā |  
dharmādharma phalā snehaṃ pūrṇavahnau juhomyahaṃ svāhā ||  
  
p. 78b)  
  
antarniraṃtara nibandhanamedhamāne māyāndhakāraparipanthini samvidagnau |  
ātmaprakāśana marīcikāśibhūmau viśvaṃ juhomi vasudhādiśi vāvasānamiti ||  
  
atha yogaḥ |  
  
taduktaṃ haṃsapāramesvaratantre kathitaṃ paramaṃ brahmaṃ yogaṃ śṛṇu   
varānane ādhāre tu gudasthāne paṅkajañca caturdalaṃ |  
  
karṇikāyāṃ sthitā yoniḥ kāmākhyāyatameśvarī aparokṣa hi kaṃdarpyamādhāre   
ca trikoṇakaṃ |  
  
p. 179a)  
  
svayaṃbhuliṅgamadhye tu paścimābhimukha priye |  
tasmāt tudvyaṅgulādūrdhvaṃ adho madhyaṃ tu dvyaṃgulaṃ ||  
  
ekāṅgulaṃ tu taṃ madhye caturaśrantrikoṇakaṃ |  
tanmadhya tu śikhi sthānan taptahāṭakaṃ saṃnibhaṃ ||  
  
bandhūka puṣpasaṃkāśa taḍillekhe ca vīsphurat |  
saptācci raśmi saṃyuktaṃ kālāgni rudragarbhakaṃ ||  
  
ādikṣakāraparyantaṃ kalādaśa samanvitaṃ |  
ayamagniḥ samūddiṣṭa sūryañca kathayāmi te ||  
  
p. 179b)  
  
vasti deśe mahābhāge madhyamā mūlamāśrite |  
sindūrasannibhambījaṃ javādāḍimasannibhaṃ ||  
  
ravistatraiva jānīyāt kalādvādaśasaṃyutaṃ |  
kalādyādvādaśabījaṃ yugmayugmaṃ sureśvari ||  
  
tanmadhye sa parāddhantu udyadāditya sannibhāṃ |  
rajaśaktirmahābhāge ravivāyu sthitaṃ jagat ||  
  
śirobinduriti khyāto manaścandra prakīrtitaṃ |  
ādībījamunmanī ca gagaṇaśca caturvidhaḥ ||  
  
p. 180a)  
  
ādibīja mahākāśaṃ nijacandraṃ mano bhavet |  
unmanī prāṇacandraśca mitrācandra vināśinī ||  
  
sarvacandramayo yogī dhyānaṃ samabhyaset tataḥ |  
oṃkārasthā śikhāsukṣmā ātmaikyāṃ cidrupāṃ kalā ||  
  
cintayantī parāvasthāṃ jihvāstadaśanan dṛḍhaṃ |  
sūkṣayā saha cātmānamekī bhūtantu cintayet ||  
  
haravaktasyaṃ saṃyogāt sā śikhā varddhayet priye |  
brahmagranthiṃ tato bhitvā kulītaṃ chinna mastayo ||  
  
p. 180b)  
  
brahmarandhre suṣumnāyāmvāyurviśatimadhyamāṃ |  
svādhisthānantato bhitvā śravaṇaṃ viśati dvayaṃ ||  
  
manipūre nābhideśe brahmaṇaḥ sadananpriye |  
dīptajyotirmayaṃ śuddhaṃ tatobhindyāt sadāgatiḥ ||  
  
tadurddhvaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ sthānaṃ nīlotpaladalaprabhaṃ |  
brahma granthiṃ hṛdibhitvā kātī dvetriguṇātmakaṃ ||  
  
dakṣakarma tato datvā tālumūlaṃ svarātmakaṃ |  
rudrālayaṃ tato bhitvā lalāṭaśca maheśvarī ||  
  
p. 181a)  
  
māheśvarī indu kalāṃ merau nirodhikāraṇam |  
śaṃkhinīmānasaṃ prāpyavāsthi śūnyavibhartisaḥ ||  
  
amṛti yadi sargasthaṃ paramānanda lakṣaṇaṃ |  
sahaśrāramahāpadmaṃ raktakiñjalkaśobhitaṃ ||  
  
drutaraktāmbuje kṣābhaṃ dhārāpāta pravarṣaṇaṃ |  
mahāsamudra madhyasthaṃ nīlaṃ kṣīramayaṃ priye ||  
  
urddhādhāre śṛṇuyatproktaṃ | tanmayodraniraṃjanaṃ ||  
  
nityānandamayī devīṃ dhyāyet tatra samāhitaḥ |  
sahaśradala padmācca pīyuṣaṃ prāpayet priye ||  
  
p. 181b)  
  
pītvā pītvā punaḥ pītvā mūlādhāre praveśayet |  
punaḥ kūlāmṛtaṃ pītvā punareva viśetkulaṃ ||  
  
devisthāne sahaśrāre prāviśedākulaṃ priye |  
dvādaśārṇa punarbhitvā yonimudrānibaṃdhanāt ||  
  
pītvā punarmūlādhāre piṃgalayā guṇadvayaṃ |  
vastinādikayormadhye udyānañca sureśvarī ||  
  
jālaṃdharaṃ tathā vaktre guḍe ca kāmarūpakaṃ |  
hṛdimadhye pūrṇagiriṃ śrīhadṛstālukopari ||  
  
p. 182a)  
  
grivau pūrṇaṃ girīpīṭhaṃ kalpodyānaṃ śirasthitaṃ |  
yejetkalpataruṃ tasmin sādhakabhiṣṭa siddhidaṃ ||  
  
dhyāye lipitarornūle devī tanmaya paṃkaje |  
vadanti sudhiyo vṛkṣaṃ nityavarṇamayaṃ priye ||  
  
sacinmaya mahābījaṃ bindunāda mahāśivaṃ |  
pṛthivyakṣara śākhābhiḥ sarvāśāṃ suvijaṃbhitaṃ ||  
  
sapāsakṣara pātraiśca saṃchādita jagatrayaṃ |  
vahni varṇāṅkulairdīptaṃ ratnairiva suradrumaḥ ||  
  
marutāṃ tulasatpuṣpai dyotayaṃ taṃ puraḥśriyāṃ |  
ākāśārṇa phalainetraṃ sarvabhūtā śriyaṃparaṃ ||  
  
p. 182b)  
  
mahāmṛtākṣamadhubhiḥ siyaṃ taṃ parameśvarīṃ |  
vedāgamādibhiḥ proktaṃ samunnati manoharaṃ ||  
  
śivaśakti mayaṃ sākṣāt chāyāśrita jagantrayaṃ |  
tanmūle bhāvayad devī sarvadeśarirīṇāṃ ||  
  
evaṃ ciṃtanamātreṇa kiṃ na siddhyaṃti bhūtale |  
  
taṃtrarājepi |  
  
sāmānya yogaprakaraṇaṃ |  
  
mūrddhāta vidyā madhyesthaṃ sudhāvarya vidhāyakaṃ |  
vibhāvayantiti nanujapedekāgra mānasaḥ ||  
  
p. 183)  
  
maṇḍalāt kavitā siddhiḥ sarvabhāṣāmapī bhavet |  
vādādīṣu ca sarvatra devatātmā jayī bhavet ||  
  
sakalajanī stotre |  
  
ānandalakṣaṇamatāhata nāsti deśe nādātmanā parigataṃ tava rūpamīḍe |  
antargatena manasā paricīyamānaṃśaṃsaṃti netra salilaiḥ pulakaiśca dhanyāḥ |  
  
upahāso na kartavyo yathā śāstra samīritaṃ |  
vidheyamasya marmajñairvīrāvaddho yamaṃjaliḥ ||  
  
p. 184)  
  
lambodarasya pautreṇa kamalakara sūnunā |  
alekhi śaṃkareṇaiṣā vāsanādi vinirṇaya ||  
  
iti śrīśaṅkarācārya viracitāyāṃ tārārahasyavṛttau taṃtracūḍāmaṇau   
vāsanānīrṇayo nāma pañcadaśamaḥ paṭalaḥ samāptam || 15 ||  
  
śubham |  
  
samvat 1957 sālamiti | roja | kṛṣṇājī |  
  
samāptam |
